CAUVERY-VAIGAI-GUNDAR LINK CANAL PROJECT, KARUR DISTRICT 
FORM VI
[See rule 16]
DECLARATION
(ந.க. ்அ1/1041/2022)
(Rc.No.A1/ 1095 /2022.)                 
No. VI(1)/608/2022.
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of  12.61.86  hectares of land is required in Mahadhanapuram 
South (Block-A) Village in Krishnarayapuram Taluk  in Karur District for a public purpose, namely, in Cauvery-Vaigai- 
Gundar Link canal Project, Karur.
Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 2.96.10 hectares is under acquisition 
for the above said project in the Mahadhanapuram South (Block-A)  Village in Krishnarayapuram Taluk in Karur District 
whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under 
Section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement 
Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013).  
The number of families likely to be resettled due to land acquisition is  09  for whom rehabilitation and resettlement 
compensation has been ﬁ xed.
Survey Numbers of Lands to be acquired 605/6 and others in Village Mahadhanapuram South   (Block-A), Taluk 
Krishnarayapuram, District  Karur, Area 2.96.10 (in hectares) Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying 
under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and minerals which may 
be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the 
land is being acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition Oﬃ  cer, Karur, Special Tahsildar (L.A), 
Unit-1, Cauvery-Vaigai-Gundar Link Canal Project, Krishnarayapuram and Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, 
Special Division, Kulithalai on any  working day.
A  Summary of the Rehabilitation and Resettlement Scheme is appended below:

2.
Land for Land
In the case of irrigation project, as far as 
possible and in lieu of compensation to 
be paid for land acquired, a minimum 
of one acre of land in the command 
area of the project for which the land 
is acquired and in case of land owner 
belonging to the Scheduled Castes or 
the Scheduled Tribes will be provided 
land equivalent to land acquired or 
two and a one-half acres, whichever is 
lower.
Not applicable, Since 
aﬀ ected 
families 
owning 
agriculture 
land and land owners 
are not belonging to 
Scheduled Castes or 
the Scheduled Tribes

project aﬀ ected families, in proportion 
to the area of their land acquired.

the land is not acquired 
for 
urbanization 
purpose, 
Nil

where

are 
created 
through the project/ one time payment 
of ﬁ ve lakhs rupees per aﬀ ected family/

primarily 
depend

to 
Land 
acquisition, 
this entitlement is not 
provided to anyone

5.
Subsistence
grant for
displaced
families for a

Each aﬀ ected family which is displaced 
from the land acquired shall be given 
a 
monthly

equivalent to three thousand rupees 
per month for a period of one year from 
the date of award.
Subsistence allowance 
of Rs. 3000/- per month 
for a period of one year 
will be given to each 
displaced family.

One-time grant

a minimum of twenty-ﬁ ve thousand 
rupees
Artisan, Small traders or

acquisition.

provided to anyone.

9.
Fishing rights
In cases of irrigation or hydel projects, 
the aﬀ ected families may be allowed 
ﬁ shing rights in the reservoirs, in such 
manner as may be prescribed by the 
appropriate Government.
There is no scope to 
ﬁ shing in this project. 
Hence, 
it 
is 
not 
applicable.
Nil

will be given to each 
displaced  family.

Stamp duty and
registration fee
(1) The stamp duty and other fees 
payable for registration of the land or 
house allotted to the aﬀ ected families 
shall be borne by the Requiring Body.
(2) it shall be free from all encumbrances
(3) it may be in the joint names of wife 
and husband of the aﬀ ected
family.
Aﬀ ected 
family 
having other land and 
equivalent 
cost 
of 
the house is oﬀ ered 
in lieu of constructed 
house, Stamp duty & 
Registration for does 
not arise.
Nil

No. VI(1)/609/2022.
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of  9.74.10  hectares of land is required in Mahadhanapuram 
South (Block-B) Village in Krishnarayapuram Taluk  in Karur District for a public purpose, namely, in Cauvery-Vaigai- 
Gundar Link Canal Project, Karur
 Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 2.91.60 hectares is under acquisition 
for the above said project in the Mahadhanapuram South (Block-B)  Village in Krishnarayapuram Taluk in Karur District 
whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under 
Section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement 
Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013).  
The number of families likely to be resettled due to land acquisition is  03  for whom rehabilitation and resettlement 
compensation has been ﬁ xed.
Survey Numbers of Lands to be acquired 384/2C and others in Village Mahadhanapuram South (Block-B), Taluk 
Krishnarayapuram, District  Karur, Area 2.91.60 (in hectares) Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying 
under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and minerals which may 
be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the 
land is being acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition oﬃ  cer,Karur, Special Tahsildar (L.A), 
Unit-1, Cauvery-Vaigai-Gundar Link Canal Project, Krishnarayapuram and Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, 
Special Division, Kulithalai on any  working day.

No. VI(1)/610/2022
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of  9.14.30  hectares of land is required in Mahadhanapuram 
South (Block-C) Village in Krishnarayapuram Taluk  in Karur District for a public purpose, namely, in Cauvery-vaigai- 
Gundar Link canal Project, Karur.
 Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 7.04.29 hectares is under acquisition 
for the above said project in the Mahadhanapuram South (Block-C)  Village in Krishnarayapuram Taluk in Karur District 
whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 
of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central 
Act 30 of 2013).  
The number of families likely to be resettled due to land acquisition is  01  for whom rehabilitation and resettlement 
compensation has been ﬁ xed.
Survey Numbers of Lands to be acquired 1350/3 and others in Village Mahadhanapuram South (Block-C), Taluk 
Krishnarayapuram, District  Karur, Area 7.04.29 (in hectares) Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the 
29


said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and minerals which may be required to 
be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition oﬃ  cer,Karur, Special Tahsildar (L.A), Unit-1, 
Cauvery-Vaigai-Gundar Link Canal Project, Krishnarayapuram and Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special 
Division, Kulithalai on any  working day.

Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of  07.02.10  hectares of land is required in Thalinji village in Kulithalai 
Taluk  in Karur District for a public purpose, namely, in Cauvery-vaigai- Gundar Link canal Project, Karur
 Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 1.41.80   hectares is under acquisition for 
the above said project in the Thalinji Village in Kulithalai Taluk in Karur District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 
of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central 
Act 30 of 2013).  
 No family is eligible for Rehabilitation and Resettlement compensation in this village.
Survey Numbers of Lands to be acquired 269/3 and others in Village Thalinji, Taluk Kulithalai, District  Karur, Area 
1.41.80 (in hectares) Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of 
the said land, except such parts of the mines and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the 
construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition oﬃ  cer, Karur, Special Tahsildar (L.A), Unit-3, 
Cauvery-Vaigai-Gundar Link Canal Project, Kulithalai and Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special Division, 
Kulithalai on any  working day.

to artisan, small

Each aﬀ ected family of an artisan, small 
trader or self-employed person or an aﬀ ected

or commercial, industrial or institutional

minimum of twenty-ﬁ ve thousand rupees
Artisan, Small traders or Self

in

acquisition.

provided to anyone.

9.
Fishing rights
In cases of irrigation or hydel projects, the 
aﬀ ected families may be allowed ﬁ shing rights 
in the reservoirs, in such manner as may be 
prescribed by the appropriate Government.
There is no scope to ﬁ shing 
in this project.  Hence, it is 
not applicable.

10.

Resettlement

Each aﬀ ected family shall be given a onetime

acquisition. 
Hence 
this 
entitlement is not provided to 
anyone.

registration fee

for registration of the land or house allotted

(2) it shall be free from all encumbrances
(3) it may be in the joint names of wife and 
husband of the aﬀ ected
family.

displaced due to this Land 
acquisition.

entitlement is not provided to

 Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of 14.72.96 hectares of land is required in Vaiganallur 
South (Block-1) village in Kulithalai Taluk in Karur District for a public purpose, namely, in Cauvery-vaigai – Gundar 
Link canal Project, Karur
 Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 3.04.26 hectares is under acquisition 
for the above said project in the Vaiganallur South (Block-1) Village in Kulithalai Taluk in Karur District whose detailed 
description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under 
section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement 
Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). 
The number of families likely to be resettled due to land acquisition is 10 for whom rehabilitation and resettlement 
compensation has been ﬁ xed.
Survey Numbers of Lands to be acquired 355/2C in Village Vaiganallur South (Block-1), Taluk Kulithalai, District 
Karur, Area 3.04.26 (in hectares) Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any 
particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and minerals which may be required to be dug or 
removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, are 
not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition oﬃ  cer, Karur, Special Tahsildar (L.A), 
Unit-2, Cauvery-Vaigai-Gundar Link Canal Project, Kulithalai and Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special 
Division, Kulithalai on any working day.

(Rc.No.A1/ 1027/2022)                
No. VI(1)/613/2022.
Whereas, it appears to the Government that a total of  13.34.17 hectares of land is required in Vaiganallur South(Block-2) 
village in Kulithalai Taluk  in Karur District for a public purpose, namely, in Cauvery-vaigai- Gundar Link canal Project, Karur
 Now, therefore, a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 06.30.03 hectares is under acquisition for 
the above said project in the Vaiganallur South(Block-2) Village in Kulithalai Taluk in Karur District whose detailed description 
is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 
of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central 
Act 30 of 2013).  
 The number of families likely to be resettled due to land acquisition is 6 for whom resettlement area has been identiﬁ ed, 
whose brief description is as follows.
Survey Numbers of Lands to be acquired 632/1V  in Village Vaiganallur South(Block-2), Taluk Kulithalai, District  Karur, 
Area  06.30.03 (in hectares) Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular 
portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used 
during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition oﬃ  cer,Karur, Special Tahsildar (L.A), Unit-2, 
Cauvery-Vaigai-Gundar Link Canal Project, Kulithalai and Executive Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Division, 
Kulithalai on any  working day.

 Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013.  
(Central Act 30/2013), Notiﬁcation for Time extension of 19(1) Declaration Under Section 19(7)
(RC.No.A1/978/2022)
No.VI(1)/614/2022.
Wherein the Government of Tamil Nadu have originally accorded sanction for acquisition of 427.81.21 Hectares of pattlands 
and Transfer of 36.20.85 Hectares of Poramboke lands in 17  Villages for implementation of Cauvery-Vaigai-Gundar Link Canal 
Project in Karur Diﬆrict as per G.O.(Ms) No.115, Public Works (N2) Department dated 30-04-2020 and G.O.(Ms) No. 169, Water 
Resources (K1) Department, dated : 26-11-2021.
Under Section 11(1) of the Act Preliminary Notiﬁcation was published for Land Acquisition in 3 Villages as liﬆed below.
Since, work has been initiated to register Land through Private Negotiation to requisition body, for Publication of declaration 
under Section 19(1) of Right to Fair compension and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act-2013, 
time extended in following Villages for a period of 12 Months with extended date for each village as mentioned in column (6) of the 
table below as per the provisions given under section 19(7) of the Act.
